<div id="review_164683958" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/164683958" />
    <a title="Natasha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2496802-natasha"><img alt="Natasha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1572201679p2/2496802.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/164683958?book_show_action=true">Apr 30, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha" href="/user/show/2496802-natasha">Natasha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer164683958" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11097216350057272086">"To the public, I’m Gin Blanco, owner of Ashland’s best barbecue joint. To my friends, I’m the Spider, retired assassin."<br/><br/>I strongly suggest you read this series in order. It shortly introduces some things you may have missed in previous novels, but it's not enough to know exactly what's going on and to appreciate the characters growth and relationships. <br/><br/>Gin Blanco will never truly be retired, but it's for the best..she really does shine when in her element. Jennifer Estep is a fantastic storytel</span>
  <span id="freeText11097216350057272086" style="display:none">"To the public, I’m Gin Blanco, owner of Ashland’s best barbecue joint. To my friends, I’m the Spider, retired assassin."<br /><br />I strongly suggest you read this series in order. It shortly introduces some things you may have missed in previous novels, but it's not enough to know exactly what's going on and to appreciate the characters growth and relationships. <br /><br />Gin Blanco will never truly be retired, but it's for the best..she really does shine when in her element. Jennifer Estep is a fantastic storyteller and her action scenes are truly engrossing. I feel as if I'm Gin, the kick-ass assassin/hero. (Gin would probably laugh if you called her a hero, but she is turning out to be a modern day Robin Hood..only instead of stealing from the rich, she usually murders them..)<br /><br />The characters in this novel are excellent. I really love Finn, Gin's best friend/adopted brother. I wish he would get his own story. He's one of those men you think will never find love because he loves every woman, but once he finds the one woman who holds his heart, he's going to be the best companion. Who else wants to see Finn gets his own story?<br /><br />Another character I loved in this novel was Owen, Gin's new love interest. I liked Donovan Caine, her previous boyfriend, but I knew he wasn't right for Gin. Owen fits Gin perfectly, he's alpha enough to support Gin when she needs it, but won't pressure her where Donovan always seemed to do. I have a feeling we haven't seen the last of Donovan, but I don't want this relationship ruined, so I wonder how it will be played out if he resurfaces in Gins life.<br /><br />A male I hate and know I'm not alone with my feelings is Elliot Slater, Mad Monroe's right hand man and terrorizer. Every time he graces the pages, I want to punch him.. although we all know how that would end. :O<br /><br />I can't forget Mab Monroe. I know she's the main villain and without her it wouldn't be the same, for now at least.. but at times I just thought, "Your a assassin Gin, snipe her from afar?" I know that would be too easy and not really eventful, but I really don't like her. <br />Yes, I know I sound very violent, wanting to punch Elliot and shoot Mab, but if you read the series you know it's just how it makes you feel. Jennifer Estep makes you so in tuned with the novel, you start thinking like Gin.. or was that just me? Ha Ha!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="11097216350057272086" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_416513087" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/416513087" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4295616-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1531866745p2/4295616.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/416513087?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/4295616-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/13423388-venom">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer416513087" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1217229958822861168">****Review will contain mild spoilers if you are not update on the series.****<br/><br/>Ok the awesomeness of this series just gets better with each book. Each book in the Elemental Assassins series has its own plot with a bigger picture plot surrounding the murder of Gin’s mother and older sister. Things keep building as Gin finds out more about that night and about her later handler, Flecter.<br/><br/>Gin is still mourning her handler and foster father, Fletcher. She is also having a hard time with her love life.</span>
  <span id="freeText1217229958822861168" style="display:none">****Review will contain mild spoilers if you are not update on the series.****<br /><br />Ok the awesomeness of this series just gets better with each book. Each book in the Elemental Assassins series has its own plot with a bigger picture plot surrounding the murder of Gin’s mother and older sister. Things keep building as Gin finds out more about that night and about her later handler, Flecter.<br /><br />Gin is still mourning her handler and foster father, Fletcher. She is also having a hard time with her love life. But as one douche bag leaves town; another HOTTER and more suited for Gin, guy comes along.<br /><br />“I don’t judge you for what you’ve done, Gin. Why are you judging me for another man’s mistakes? Because Donovan Caine did make a mistake,” Owen said in a soft voice. “Letting someone like you go.”<br /><br />By the time Venom ends I can’t see a more perfect guy for Gin than Owen.<br /><br />Gin just can’t seem to stay retired from the assassin gig. But instead of getting paid for her skills she is using them as a service to the good people of Ashland.<br /><br />“I’m just wondering how exactly I went from being the Spider to the Robin fucking Hood of the greater Ashland area... Instead of stealing from the rich, I’m stabbing them to death for the poor.”<br /><br />Gin and gang has their hands full trying to help Rosyln Phillips with a stalker problem. The stalker in question is Elliot Slater, Mab Monroe’s head of security. Gin has no problem planning a way to kill the giant, since we start out Venom with Slater beating the crap out of Gin on the college campus. How can that be? Gin decides to go along with the beating as not to give away her cover as Gin Blanco.<br /><br />Gin spends a great deal of Venom protecting her cover in order to get closer to Mab Monroe and figuring out a way to take her out for killing her family all those years ago.<br /><br />Speaking of family, Gin finally gets to meet her baby sister that she thought died with her other sister and mother on that dark night. Gin and baby sister Bria are on different sides of the law but are more alike than either would have guessed.<br /><br />Venom is full of action, mystery and a healthy dose of dark humor and snark. I love the world and characters that Jennifer Estep has built. It’s been a while since a series has grabbed me the way this one has.<br /><br />And now that I’m done with this review and can now start Tangled Threads!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1217229958822861168" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13244951186162023385">Gin's still trying to settle into retirement but how can she do that when her friends need her? Turns out Roslyn the vampire is having problems with Mab's giant, Elliot Slater, and since Gin feels responsible, she can't say no. <br/><br/>I loved how things are all starting to come together. The "family" is really meshing well, Bria's in the picture, Gin's love life took a turn for the better AND Gin's finally making her move against Mab ~ and what a move it was! <br/><br/>Gin is her fabulous self and I like that sh</span>
  <span id="freeText13244951186162023385" style="display:none">Gin's still trying to settle into retirement but how can she do that when her friends need her? Turns out Roslyn the vampire is having problems with Mab's giant, Elliot Slater, and since Gin feels responsible, she can't say no. <br /><br />I loved how things are all starting to come together. The "family" is really meshing well, Bria's in the picture, Gin's love life took a turn for the better AND Gin's finally making her move against Mab ~ and what a move it was! <br /><br />Gin is her fabulous self and I like that she is really starting to believe in her powers. That's the part that has been bothering me and while I know she has some stuff to get through, I just want her to get on with it!! <br /><br />And hellloooo Owen. All I can say is I know why all my friends love him. We get to know him a lot better and I love the history between him and Gin. But I have a feeling that we haven't seen the last of Donovan.<br /><br />All the characters were really great...I just love the whole family thing. Finn is being his typical self but he really steps up to the plate when he needs to and even goes beyond what is expected. His Dad would be sooo proud. Jo-Jo was amazing as always and Sophia...I loved seeing the little cracks opening up. Roslyn and Xavier seem to becoming bigger players and I was glad that things got more settled between Gin and Roslyn. And that leaves Bria...I love all the baby steps and I can't wait for some clues to fall into place! <br /><br />And the giants? Ee<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www...they">www...they</a> really creeped me out especially Slater (but not Xavier of course). I really, REALLY loved what happened to Slater...especially after what he did to Gin the first time! <br /><br />I can understand why people say this is when the series gets good. The story had a good pace with lots of interesting things happened. I loved the shower scene! Owen was sooo sweet! I can't wait for the next book!<br /><br /><br />Favorite quotes: <br /><br />♦ "I'm not most men."<br /><br />♦ “That’s hard core, Gin,” Finn replied. “Very hard core. Kind of kinky too.” A grim smile tightened my lips. “That’s me. Gin Blanco. Hard core and kinky to the bitter end.”<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6628992374300721562">Gin Blanco is a (sort of retired) assassin who's life is blowing wide open. Truths revealed, new possibilities forming, and a whole lot of action going on.<br/><br/><br/><br/>I LOVE this series. I love that it's dark and gritty and that Gin sees herself as this hard shell of a woman when the reality is that she's fierce and loyal and protects those she cares for or makes promises to. It's not sunshine and roses here in assassin land, but I really liked that this book shows us Gin opening up a bit, her circle expand</span>
  <span id="freeText6628992374300721562" style="display:none">Gin Blanco is a (sort of retired) assassin who's life is blowing wide open. Truths revealed, new possibilities forming, and a whole lot of action going on.<br /><br /><br /><br />I LOVE this series. I love that it's dark and gritty and that Gin sees herself as this hard shell of a woman when the reality is that she's fierce and loyal and protects those she cares for or makes promises to. It's not sunshine and roses here in assassin land, but I really liked that this book shows us Gin opening up a bit, her circle expanding and some glimmers of hope for a real future shining through. <br /><br /><br /><br />Gin doesn't rely on magic and tricks to kick ass - she has mad skills too. There's a lot of rules to know (about the people of her world, how things work, etc) so DO NOT try to read out of order. While I found the book a satisfying installment in this series it's really not stand-alone. <br /><br /><br /><br />It's fast paced, told from Gin's point of view, and I literally could not put it down. Estep brought her A-game once again to this book and I loved every single page. It was everything I hoped for and more. Counting the months until #4 releases... <br /><br /><br /><br />note: author has good website info, seen here: <a target="_blank" href="http://www.jenniferestep.com/books-series/elemental-assassin-series" title="http://www.jenniferestep.com/books-series/elemental-assassin-series" rel="nofollow noopener">http://www.jenniferestep.com/books-serie...</a> </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1083908174" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13869341220038167726">Why have I been neglecting to read this series?! This installment was enough to bump Gin Blanco to my list of favorite series. Full review coming. </span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3017802027" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6301615562269059668">Gin's story continues where we left off in the previous book, with her retired from her lucrative assassin's career, yet still utilizing her skills, only this time to help people.<br/><br/>In this part, she is dealing with the ripples her actions in the previous book cost, namely, the vampire Roslyn coming to the attention of Elliot Slater, the big bad Mab Monroe's pet goon. Elliot is a psycho who is stalking Roslyn, who is reaching the end of her rope, and Gin, who feels guilty for her role in the situat</span>
  <span id="freeText6301615562269059668" style="display:none">Gin's story continues where we left off in the previous book, with her retired from her lucrative assassin's career, yet still utilizing her skills, only this time to help people.<br /><br />In this part, she is dealing with the ripples her actions in the previous book cost, namely, the vampire Roslyn coming to the attention of Elliot Slater, the big bad Mab Monroe's pet goon. Elliot is a psycho who is stalking Roslyn, who is reaching the end of her rope, and Gin, who feels guilty for her role in the situation, vows to help her get rid of Elliot.<br /><br />Gin has also finally found her long lost sister, Bria, who has recently moved to the area and taken over detective Donovan Caine's duties. Bria is pretty kick ass herself, but she operates on the right side of the law, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[so Gin does not reveal her true identity, but is more than happy for the opportunity to get to know the woman her sister has grown into <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />Another thing that's changed is Gin's love life. She might have been hesitant at first, but Owen slowly wore down her defenses, with his acceptance of her more than anything else. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Gin ends up telling him the truth about who she really is, and instead of turning away, as she believed he would, he in turn reveals that she had once saved his and his beloved sister's lives when they were kids and that he had been trying to find a way to repay her ever since their paths crossed again <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br /><br />Owen is a huge improvement over Donovan, who was one of the main reasons why I wasn't thrilled with the first book of the series. I am glad he is out of the picture and I'm looking forward to seeing how Gin and Owen's relationship develops.<br /><br />By the end of this book Gin <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[or rather the Spider, has taken out Mab's right hand man and declared war on her <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, setting up the stage for what's to come in future books. <br /><br />The next book in the series is <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8675994.Tangled_Threads__Elemental_Assassin___4_" title="Tangled Threads (Elemental Assassin, #4) by Jennifer Estep" rel="nofollow noopener">Tangled Threads</a>, but I might read the short stories I skipped so far before getting to it, since it looks like they might give some valuable insight into Gin and her loved ones.<br /><br /><i>Previous book reviews:</i><br />✦ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/599043645" rel="nofollow noopener">Web of Lies (Elemental Assassin, #2)</a> ~ ★★★ (19/10/2019)<br />✦ <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/123731930" rel="nofollow noopener">Spider's Bite (Elemental Assassin #1)</a> ~ ★★★ (25/04/2013)</span>

I admire most everything about her - her grit, courage, intelligence, passion, tenacity, mad skills, and mostly her deep and abiding care she has for the people she loves.   <span id="freeText1731124808865922474" style="display:none">This series just gets better and better. I can't believe how emotionally invested I've become in Gin Blanco. I've said it before, Gin and I could be besties. I admire most everything about her - her grit, courage, intelligence, passion, tenacity, mad skills, and mostly her deep and abiding care she has for the people she loves. I find this book emotional and darn frustrating because they are going to take that one issue and extended to the next book. Please, please, let this issue get resolved soon because I do not think my heart can take it!</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3081816818" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6058291656760138776">Such great characters! I really love Gin and the host of secondary characters in her world. There is a bit too much rehashing of previous books and I still don't believe she would have fallen for Donovan so hard, so quickly that she's still rehashing his leaving. It was good to see her seem to finally put that behind her and move forward. A lot happens in this book and I love the way the overall plot is moving. Can't wait for the next one.</span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('pK3ZdKo9kzbS7gJqwWPM7Eo3Eom1NaH3JS4x8qk8naCy8Pe+i0l9wDL7DUXRxaOA4AR+TaBBjKsuwKCJn/ofmw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('iQFIYvUT28qgAdx+jg/f51ErvPyg0wXOqt2mtwopvSCfXGao1Gc1PEAU01GeqbCL+xjQOLWnKJKhMzfMPO8/Gw==')})
  }

  <span id="freeText3458880533573978250" style="display:none">Jennifer Estep is a New York Times, USA Today, and international bestselling author, prowling the streets of her imagination in search of her next fantasy idea. She has written more than 40 books, along with numerous novellas and stories.<br /><br />In her spare time, Jennifer enjoys hanging out with friends and family, doing yoga, and reading fantasy and romance books.
